The Company posted quarterly revenue of $64 billion, an increase of 2 percent from the year-ago quarter, and quarterly earnings per diluted share of $3.03, up 4 percent. International sales accounted for 60 percent of the quarter&#8217;s revenue.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:9pt;">&#8220;We concluded a groundbreaking fiscal 2019 with our highest Q4 revenue ever, fueled by accelerating growth from Services, Wearables and iPad,&#8221; said Tim Cook, Apple&#8217;s CEO. &#8220;With customers and reviewers raving about the new generation of iPhones, today&#8217;s debut of new, noise-cancelling AirPods Pro, the hotly-anticipated arrival of Apple TV+ just two days away, and our best lineup of products and services ever, we&#8217;re very optimistic about what the holiday quarter has in store.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:Helvetica,sans-serif;font-size:9pt;">&#8220;Our strong business performance drove record Q4 EPS of $3.03 and record Q4 operating cash flow of $19.9 billion,&#8221;
